## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate kernel in /workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p33/optimization_rounds/round1/output_model_new.py

Use MFMA instructions `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` to do matrix multiplications and loads the data from global memory using vectorized loads S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4. The MFMA instruction computes 32x32x8 matmul cooperatively in a wave. Build larger tiles by issuing multiple MFMA instructions across K and output subtiles.
  
MFMA swizzle invariants:
  For A, `i in [0,32)`, `j in [0,8)`: `A(i, j) -> (lane_id = i + (j / 4) * 32, element = j % 4)`
  For B, `j in [0,8)`, `i in [0,32)`: `B(j, i) -> (lane_id = j + (i / 4) * 32, element = i % 4)`

Accumulator invariant for C: for each lane in [0, 64) and acc_idx in [0, 16):
  - col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
  - row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)

Do not invent a different unpacking. Do not use a naive acc_idx -> contiguous row mapping. Treat this mapping as fixed when writing results.

Stage A and B through LDS. Each thread loads operand fragments in 16-byte chunks. Treat each 16-byte fragment as `(4, S.u32)` and reinterpret it as `2 x (4, S.bf16)`. Feed both `(4, S.bf16)` halves into MFMA in natural order. The intended effect is a cooperative `32x32x16` accumulation from two natural MFMA steps. Do not add lane-dependent or K-dependent control flow to select halves.
  - The two `(4, S.bf16)` halves from one 16-byte LDS load collectively represent a swizzled `32x16` operand contribution with 4-column interleaving.
  - Consuming them in natural order must produce the same final C as a naive conceptual layout because operand pairings remain consistent under MFMA swizzle.

Scale the kernel from one wave to four waves without changing the MFMA per-wave invariant. Interpret the 4 warps as a 2 x 2 warp grid. Keep MFMA math identical per warp. Only add warp ownership offsets at operand fetch and output writeback.

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S
SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951

def _launch():
    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
BATCH_SIZE = 1024
IN_FEATURES = 8192
OUT_FEATURES = 8192
EPS = 1e-05

@substrate.jit
def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16), W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16), BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), SCALE: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16), Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16)):
    for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
        for j in S.range(OUT_FEATURES):
            acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for kk in S.range(IN_FEATURES):
                acc += S.convert(X[i, kk], S.f32) * S.convert(W[kk, j], S.f32)
            Y[i, j] = S.convert((acc + S.convert(BIAS0[j], S.f32)) * S.convert(SCALE[j], S.f32), S.bf16)
    for j in S.range(OUT_FEATURES):
        mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
            mean += S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32)
        mean = mean / S.convert(BATCH_SIZE, S.f32)
        var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
            d = S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32) - mean
            var += d * d
        var = var / S.convert(BATCH_SIZE, S.f32)
        denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
            v = (S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32) - mean) / denom
            v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[j], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[j], S.f32)
            Y[i, j] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

class ModelNew(nn.Module):

    def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, scale_shape, eps=1e-05, momentum=0.1):
        super().__init__()
        self.gemm = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
        self.scale = nn.Parameter(torch.randn(scale_shape))
        self.bn = nn.BatchNorm1d(out_features, eps=eps, momentum=momentum)

    def forward(self, x):
        if tuple(x.shape) != (BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES) or x.dtype != torch.bfloat16 or tuple(self.scale.shape) != (OUT_FEATURES,) or (self.bn.eps != EPS):
            raise RuntimeError('This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.')
        w_t = self.gemm.weight.t().to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        bias = self.gemm.bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        scale = self.scale.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        bn_w = self.bn.weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        bn_b = self.bn.bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
        fused_kernel[_launch](x.contiguous(), w_t, bias, scale, bn_w, bn_b, y)
        return y

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_16x16x16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
import _substrate_bindings as _C
from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip(
    src: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    dst: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)
    dst_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(dst, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    offset_x2 = S.convert(4, S.i32)
    offset_x4 = S.convert(12, S.i32)

    value_x1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x1(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    value_x2 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x2(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    value_x4 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)

    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x1(value_x1, dst_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x2(value_x2, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x4(value_x4, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view(
    src: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    dst: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    frag = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    for i in S.range(2):
        for j in S.range(4):
            dst[i * 4 + j] = frag[i, j, 0]


def generate_mlir(jit_fn) -> str:
    jit_deps = _collect_jit_dependencies(jit_fn)
    import_module = _build_import_module([jit_fn, *jit_deps])

    generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
    generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)

    for dep in jit_deps:
        dep_func = _get_function_def(dep.parse())
        generator.visit_function_def(dep_func, "[]", "jit")

    kernel_func = _get_function_def(jit_fn.parse())
    generator.visit_function_def(kernel_func, "[]", "kernel")
    return generator.get_mlir()


@unittest.skipUnless(
    has_rocm(),
    "Requires ROCm/HIP with an AMD GPU.",
)
class TestAMDGPUBufferOps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_raw_buffer_roundtrip(self):
        src = torch.arange(7, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda") * 17 - 9
        dst = torch.full((7,), -1, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_make_rsrc_generates_pointer_and_range(self):
        mlir = generate_mlir(kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip)

        self.assertIn(
            "substrate.memref.extract_aligned_pointer_as_index",
            mlir,
        )
        self.assertGreaterEqual(mlir.count("vector.insert %arg2"), 2, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_load"), 3, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_store"), 3, mlir)

    def test_raw_buffer_bf16_view_extract(self):
        src = torch.randn((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        dst = torch.zeros((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_subview_view_offsets(result: S.Tensor((2,), S.u32)):
    shared_words = S.make_shared((16,), S.u32)
    left_words = S.subview(shared_words, (0,), (8,), (1,))
    right_words = S.subview(shared_words, (8,), (8,), (1,))
    layout = S.make_layout((2, 2), (2, 1))
    left = S.view(left_words, S.u32, layout)
    right = S.view(right_words, S.u32, layout)

    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    if tid == 0:
        left[0, 0] = S.convert(11, S.u32)
        right[0, 0] = S.convert(22, S.u32)

    S.syncthreads()

    if tid == 0:
        result[0] = left[0, 0]
        result[1] = right[0, 0]


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shm_subview_view_mixed_types(result: S.Tensor((4,), S.i32)):
    shared_words = S.make_shared((32,), S.u32)
    stats_words = S.subview(shared_words, (0,), (8,), (1,))
    q_words = S.subview(shared_words, (8,), (8,), (1,))
    kv_words = S.subview(shared_words, (16,), (8,), (1,))
    score_words = S.subview(shared_words, (24,), (8,), (1,))
    layout_f32 = S.make_layout((2, 4), (4, 1))
    layout_bf16 = S.make_layout((2, 4), (4, 1))
    layout_u32 = S.make_layout((2, 2), (2, 1))
    stats = S.view(stats_words, S.f32, layout_f32)
    q = S.view(q_words, S.bf16, layout_bf16)
    kv = S.view(kv_words, S.bf16, layout_bf16)
    score = S.view(score_words, S.f32, layout_f32)
    q_u32 = S.view(q_words, S.u32, layout_u32)
    kv_u32 = S.view(kv_words, S.u32, layout_u32)

    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    if tid == 0:
        stats[0, 0] = S.convert(3.0, S.f32)
        score[0, 0] = S.convert(4.0, S.f32)
        q[0, 0] = S.convert(1.0, S.bf16)
        q[0, 1] = S.convert(2.0, S.bf16)
        kv[0, 0] = S.convert(3.0, S.bf16)
        kv[0, 1] = S.convert(4.0, S.bf16)

    S.syncthreads()

    if tid == 0:
        result[0] = S.convert(stats[0, 0], S.i32)
        result[1] = q_u32[0, 0]
        result[2] = kv_u32[0, 0]
        result[3] = S.convert(score[0, 0], S.i32)

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import _substrate_bindings as _C
import substrate
import substrate.language as S

from substrate.compiler import code_generator as cg
from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)
from substrate.compiler.compiler import ASTSource


@substrate.jit
def kernel_with_num_warps(
    x: S.Tensor((1,), S.i32),
    BLOCK_SIZE: S.constexpr,
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    if tid < BLOCK_SIZE:
        x[tid] = x[tid]


class TestNumWarps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_amdgpu_llvm_ir_overrides_flat_workgroup_size_when_num_warps_set(self):
        src = ASTSource(
            kernel_with_num_warps,
            {"x": "*i32", "BLOCK_SIZE": "constexpr"},
            constexprs={"BLOCK_SIZE": {"type": "i32", "value": 16}},
        )
        constexprs_json = cg._serialize_constexprs(src)

        generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
        import_module = _build_import_module(
            [kernel_with_num_warps, *_collect_jit_dependencies(kernel_with_num_warps)]
        )
        generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)
        generator.visit_function_def(
            _get_function_def(kernel_with_num_warps.parse()), constexprs_json, "kernel"
        )

        llvm_ir = generator.get_llvm_ir("amdgcn-amd-amdhsa", "gfx90a", 2, 3)
        self.assertIn('"amdgpu-flat-work-group-size"="1,192"', llvm_ir)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

+def gemm_scale_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    SCALE: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    warp_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((BLOCK_M, 2, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((BLOCK_K, 8, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            for w in S.range(4):
+                a_words[a_row, a_half, w] = a_pack[w]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            for w in S.range(4):
+                b_words[b_row, b_seg, w] = b_pack[w]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_row_local = warp_row * 32 + (lane & 31)
+        a_group = lane >> 5
+
+        b_k = lane & 7
+        b_quad = lane >> 3
+        b_seg0 = warp_col * 4 + b_quad
+
+        a_packed = S.full((4,), S.convert(0, S.u32), S.u32)
+        b_packed = S.full((4,), S.convert(0, S.u32), S.u32)
+
+        for w in S.range(2):
+            a_packed[w] = a_words[a_row_local, 0, a_group * 2 + w]
+            a_packed[w + 2] = a_words[a_row_local, 1, a_group * 2 + w]
+            b_packed[w] = b_words[b_k, b_seg0, w]
+            b_packed[w + 2] = b_words[b_k + 8, b_seg0, w]
+
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = warp_col_base + lane_col
+        out_row = warp_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+        if out_row < BATCH_SIZE and out_col < OUT_FEATURES:
+            v = (acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)) * S.convert(SCALE[out_col], S.f32)
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def bn_stats_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    VAR: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+):
+    col = S.block_id(0) * 256 + S.thread_id(0)
+    if col < OUT_FEATURES:
         mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            mean += S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32)
+        for row in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
+            mean += S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
         mean = mean / S.convert(BATCH_SIZE, S.f32)
         var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            d = S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32) - mean
+        for row in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
+            d = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - mean
             var += d * d
-        var = var / S.convert(BATCH_SIZE, S.f32)
+        VAR[col] = var / S.convert(BATCH_SIZE, S.f32)
+        MEAN[col] = mean
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    VAR: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1) * 4 + (tid >> 6)
+    col = S.block_id(0) * 64 + (tid & 63)
+    if row < BATCH_SIZE and col < OUT_FEATURES:
+        mean = MEAN[col]
+        var = VAR[col]
         denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            v = (S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32) - mean) / denom
-            v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[j], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[j], S.f32)
-            Y[i, j] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+        v = (S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - mean) / denom
+        v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

+def gemm_scale_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    SCALE: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    warp_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((BLOCK_M, 2, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((BLOCK_K, 8, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            for w in S.range(4):
+                a_words[a_row, a_half, w] = a_pack[w]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            for w in S.range(4):
+                b_words[b_row, b_seg, w] = b_pack[w]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_row_local = warp_row * 32 + (lane & 31)
+        a_group = lane >> 5
+
+        b_k = lane & 7
+        b_quad = lane >> 3
+        b_seg0 = warp_col * 4 + b_quad
+
+        a_packed = S.full((4,), S.convert(0, S.u32), S.u32)

+        for w in S.range(2):

+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    SCALE: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    warp_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((BLOCK_M, 2, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((BLOCK_K, 8, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            for w in S.range(4):
+                a_words[a_row, a_half, w] = a_pack[w]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            for w in S.range(4):
+                b_words[b_row, b_seg, w] = b_pack[w]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_row_local = warp_row * 32 + (lane & 31)
+        a_group = lane >> 5
+
+        b_k = lane & 7
+        b_quad = lane >> 3
+        b_seg0 = warp_col * 4 + b_quad
+
+        a_packed = S.full((4,), S.convert(0, S.u32), S.u32)
+        b_packed = S.full((4,), S.convert(0, S.u32), S.u32)
+
+        for w in S.range(2):
+            a_packed[w] = a_words[a_row_local, 0, a_group * 2 + w]
+            a_packed[w + 2] = a_words[a_row_local, 1, a_group * 2 + w]
+            b_packed[w] = b_words[b_k, b_seg0, w]
+            b_packed[w + 2] = b_words[b_k + 8, b_seg0, w]
+
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = warp_col_base + lane_col
+        out_row = warp_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+        if out_row < BATCH_SIZE and out_col < OUT_FEATURES:
+            v = (acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)) * S.convert(SCALE[out_col], S.f32)
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def bn_stats_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    VAR: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+):
+    col = S.block_id(0) * 256 + S.thread_id(0)
+    if col < OUT_FEATURES:
         mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            mean += S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32)
+        for row in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
+            mean += S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
         mean = mean / S.convert(BATCH_SIZE, S.f32)
         var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            d = S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32) - mean
+        for row in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
+            d = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - mean
             var += d * d
-        var = var / S.convert(BATCH_SIZE, S.f32)
+        VAR[col] = var / S.convert(BATCH_SIZE, S.f32)
+        MEAN[col] = mean
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    VAR: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1) * 4 + (tid >> 6)
+    col = S.block_id(0) * 64 + (tid & 63)
+    if row < BATCH_SIZE and col < OUT_FEATURES:
+        mean = MEAN[col]
+        var = VAR[col]
         denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            v = (S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32) - mean) / denom
-            v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[j], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[j], S.f32)
-            Y[i, j] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+        v = (S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - mean) / denom
+        v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

+def gemm_scale_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    SCALE: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    warp_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)
+
+    a_words = S.make_shared((BLOCK_M, 2, 4), S.u32)
+    b_words = S.make_shared((BLOCK_K, 8, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            for w in S.range(4):
+                a_words[a_row, a_half, w] = a_pack[w]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            for w in S.range(4):
+                b_words[b_row, b_seg, w] = b_pack[w]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        a_row_local = warp_row * 32 + (lane & 31)
+        a_group = lane >> 5
+
+        b_k = lane & 7
+        b_quad = lane >> 3
+        b_seg0 = warp_col * 4 + b_quad
+
+        a_packed = S.full((4,), S.convert(0, S.u32), S.u32)
+        b_packed = S.full((4,), S.convert(0, S.u32), S.u32)
+
+        for w in S.range(2):
+            a_packed[w] = a_words[a_row_local, 0, a_group * 2 + w]
+            a_packed[w + 2] = a_words[a_row_local, 1, a_group * 2 + w]
+            b_packed[w] = b_words[b_k, b_seg0, w]
+            b_packed[w + 2] = b_words[b_k + 8, b_seg0, w]
+
+        m_a = S.view(a_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = warp_col_base + lane_col
+        out_row = warp_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+        if out_row < BATCH_SIZE and out_col < OUT_FEATURES:
+            v = (acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)) * S.convert(SCALE[out_col], S.f32)
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_stats_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    VAR: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),

+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),

+):

+    col = S.block_id(0) * 64 + (tid & 63)
+    if row < BATCH_SIZE and col < OUT_FEATURES:
+        mean = MEAN[col]
+        var = VAR[col]

-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):

codex
The lowering error is from building ad hoc packed vectors in registers. I’m changing the LDS layout so each lane reads a prepacked 16-byte fragment directly from shared memory, which is closer to the example and removes the cast issue.
apply patch

+def gemm_scale_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),

+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    warp_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32

+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)

+    b_lane_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            a_warp_row = a_row >> 5
+            a_lane_row = a_row & 31
+            a_lane_hi = a_lane_row + 32
+            if a_half == 0:

+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, 1] = a_pack[1]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, 0] = a_pack[2]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, 1] = a_pack[3]
+            else:
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, 2] = a_pack[0]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, 3] = a_pack[1]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, 2] = a_pack[2]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, 3] = a_pack[3]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3

+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            b_warp_col = b_seg >> 2
+            b_local_seg = b_seg & 3
+            b_lane_base = (b_row & 7) + (b_local_seg << 4)
+            b_lane0 = b_lane_base

+            if b_row < 8:
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane0, 0] = b_pack[0]
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane0, 1] = b_pack[1]

+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        m_a = S.view(a_lane_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_lane_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)

+        S.syncthreads()

+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5

+    a_lane_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_lane_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            a_warp_row = a_row >> 5
+            a_lane_row = a_row & 31
+            a_lane_hi = a_lane_row + 32
+            if a_half == 0:
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, 0] = a_pack[0]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, 1] = a_pack[1]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, 0] = a_pack[2]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, 1] = a_pack[3]
+            else:
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, 2] = a_pack[0]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, 3] = a_pack[1]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, 2] = a_pack[2]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, 3] = a_pack[3]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            b_warp_col = b_seg >> 2
+            b_local_seg = b_seg & 3
+            b_lane_base = (b_row & 7) + (b_local_seg << 4)
+            b_lane0 = b_lane_base
+            b_lane1 = b_lane_base + 8
+            if b_row < 8:
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane0, 0] = b_pack[0]
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane0, 1] = b_pack[1]
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane1, 0] = b_pack[2]
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane1, 1] = b_pack[3]
+            else:
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane0, 2] = b_pack[0]
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane0, 3] = b_pack[1]
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane1, 2] = b_pack[2]
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane1, 3] = b_pack[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        m_a = S.view(a_lane_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_lane_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = warp_col_base + lane_col
+        out_row = warp_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+        if out_row < BATCH_SIZE and out_col < OUT_FEATURES:
+            v = (acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)) * S.convert(SCALE[out_col], S.f32)
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def bn_stats_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    VAR: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+):
+    col = S.block_id(0) * 256 + S.thread_id(0)
+    if col < OUT_FEATURES:
         mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            mean += S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32)
+        for row in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
+            mean += S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)
         mean = mean / S.convert(BATCH_SIZE, S.f32)
         var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            d = S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32) - mean
+        for row in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
+            d = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - mean
             var += d * d
-        var = var / S.convert(BATCH_SIZE, S.f32)
+        VAR[col] = var / S.convert(BATCH_SIZE, S.f32)
+        MEAN[col] = mean
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    VAR: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1) * 4 + (tid >> 6)
+    col = S.block_id(0) * 64 + (tid & 63)
+    if row < BATCH_SIZE and col < OUT_FEATURES:
+        mean = MEAN[col]
+        var = VAR[col]
         denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            v = (S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32) - mean) / denom
-            v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[j], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[j], S.f32)

+        v = (S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - mean) / denom
+        v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

+        bn_b = self._cached_contiguous("bn_b", self.bn.bias)
+
+        gemm_out = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        mean = torch.empty((OUT_FEATURES,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
+        var = torch.empty((OUT_FEATURES,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
+        out = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+
+        gemm_scale_mfma_kernel[_launch_gemm](x_in, w_t, bias, scale, gemm_out, X_RANGE_BYTES, W_RANGE_BYTES)
+        bn_stats_kernel[_launch_bn_stats](gemm_out, mean, var)
+        bn_apply_kernel[_launch_bn_apply](gemm_out, mean, var, bn_w, bn_b, out)
+        return out

+def gemm_scale_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    SCALE: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    warp_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)
+
+    a_lane_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+    b_lane_words = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            a_warp_row = a_row >> 5
+            a_lane_row = a_row & 31
+            a_lane_hi = a_lane_row + 32
+            if a_half == 0:
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, 0] = a_pack[0]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, 1] = a_pack[1]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, 0] = a_pack[2]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, 1] = a_pack[3]
+            else:
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, 2] = a_pack[0]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, 3] = a_pack[1]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, 2] = a_pack[2]
+                a_lane_words[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, 3] = a_pack[3]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            b_warp_col = b_seg >> 2
+            b_local_seg = b_seg & 3
+            b_lane_base = (b_row & 7) + (b_local_seg << 4)
+            b_lane0 = b_lane_base
+            b_lane1 = b_lane_base + 8
+            if b_row < 8:
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane0, 0] = b_pack[0]
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane0, 1] = b_pack[1]
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane1, 0] = b_pack[2]
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane1, 1] = b_pack[3]
+            else:
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane0, 2] = b_pack[0]
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane0, 3] = b_pack[1]
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane1, 2] = b_pack[2]
+                b_lane_words[b_warp_col, b_lane1, 3] = b_pack[3]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        m_a = S.view(a_lane_words[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_lane_words[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = warp_col_base + lane_col
+        out_row = warp_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+        if out_row < BATCH_SIZE and out_col < OUT_FEATURES:
+            v = (acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)) * S.convert(SCALE[out_col], S.f32)
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_stats_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    VAR: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+):

+    if col < OUT_FEATURES:
         mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            mean += S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32)
+        for row in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
+            mean += S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32)

         var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            d = S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32) - mean
+        for row in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
+            d = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - mean
             var += d * d
-        var = var / S.convert(BATCH_SIZE, S.f32)
+        VAR[col] = var / S.convert(BATCH_SIZE, S.f32)
+        MEAN[col] = mean

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    VAR: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),

+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):

+    row = S.block_id(1) * 4 + (tid >> 6)
+    col = S.block_id(0) * 64 + (tid & 63)
+    if row < BATCH_SIZE and col < OUT_FEATURES:
+        mean = MEAN[col]
+        var = VAR[col]
         denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            v = (S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32) - mean) / denom
-            v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[j], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[j], S.f32)
-            Y[i, j] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+        v = (S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - mean) / denom
+        v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

+def gemm_scale_mfma_kernel(

+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63

codex
I found the likely issue: the B-fragment lane ownership was keyed off K instead of the output column. I’m repacking the LDS fragments so `lane % 32` tracks the output column on both operands, then I’ll rerun the fixed harness command.

+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            a_warp_row = a_row >> 5
+            a_lane_row = a_row & 31
+            a_lane_hi = a_lane_row + 32
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e, 0]
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e + 4, 0]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_warp_col = b_seg >> 2
+            b_local_seg = b_seg & 3
+            b_lane_base = b_local_seg * 8
+            b_lane_group = b_row >> 2
+            b_lane_off = (b_row & 3) + (b_lane_group & 1) * 4
+            b_frag_half = b_lane_group >> 1
+            for e in S.range(8):
+                b_lane = b_lane_base + e
+                b_lane_frags[b_warp_col, b_lane, b_frag_half * 4 + b_lane_off] = b_frag[e, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        m_a = S.view(a_lane_frags[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_lane_frags[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = warp_col_base + lane_col
+        out_row = warp_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+        if out_row < BATCH_SIZE and out_col < OUT_FEATURES:
+            v = (acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)) * S.convert(SCALE[out_col], S.f32)
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

 EPS = 1e-05
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WARP_SIZE = 64

+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // 64, BATCH_SIZE // 4, 1), (256, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_scale_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    SCALE: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    warp_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)
+
+    a_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            a_warp_row = a_row >> 5
+            a_lane_row = a_row & 31
+            a_lane_hi = a_lane_row + 32
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e, 0]
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e + 4, 0]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_warp_col = b_seg >> 2
+            b_local_seg = b_seg & 3
+            b_lane_base = b_local_seg * 8
+            b_lane_group = b_row >> 2
+            b_lane_off = (b_row & 3) + (b_lane_group & 1) * 4
+            b_frag_half = b_lane_group >> 1
+            for e in S.range(8):

+                b_lane_frags[b_warp_col, b_lane, b_frag_half * 4 + b_lane_off] = b_frag[e, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+

+        m_b = S.view(b_lane_frags[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)

 import torch.nn as nn
 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S
-SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951
 
-def _launch():
-    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
+
+SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951
 BATCH_SIZE = 1024
 IN_FEATURES = 8192
 OUT_FEATURES = 8192
 EPS = 1e-05
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+A_TILE_RANGE_BYTES = BLOCK_M * BLOCK_K * 2
+B_TILE_RANGE_BYTES = BLOCK_K * BLOCK_N * 2
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2
+
+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_bn_stats():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // 256, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_bn_apply():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // 64, BATCH_SIZE // 4, 1), (256, 1, 1))
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_scale_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    SCALE: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    warp_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)
+
+    a_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            a_warp_row = a_row >> 5
+            a_lane_row = a_row & 31
+            a_lane_hi = a_lane_row + 32
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e, 0]
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e + 4, 0]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_warp_col = b_seg >> 2
+            b_local_seg = b_seg & 3
+            b_lane_base = b_local_seg * 8
+            b_lane_group = b_row >> 2
+            b_lane_off = (b_row & 3) + (b_lane_group & 1) * 4
+            b_frag_half = b_lane_group >> 1
+            for e in S.range(8):
+                b_lane = b_lane_base + e
+                b_lane_frags[b_warp_col, b_lane, b_frag_half * 4 + b_lane_off] = b_frag[e, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        m_a = S.view(a_lane_frags[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_lane_frags[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = warp_col_base + lane_col
+        out_row = warp_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+        if out_row < BATCH_SIZE and out_col < OUT_FEATURES:
+            v = (acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)) * S.convert(SCALE[out_col], S.f32)
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

+def bn_stats_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),

         var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            d = S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32) - mean

+            d = S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - mean

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    VAR: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1) * 4 + (tid >> 6)
+    col = S.block_id(0) * 64 + (tid & 63)
+    if row < BATCH_SIZE and col < OUT_FEATURES:
+        mean = MEAN[col]
+        var = VAR[col]
         denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            v = (S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32) - mean) / denom
-            v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[j], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[j], S.f32)
-            Y[i, j] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+        v = (S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - mean) / denom
+        v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_scale_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    SCALE: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    warp_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)
+
+    a_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            a_warp_row = a_row >> 5
+            a_lane_row = a_row & 31
+            a_lane_hi = a_lane_row + 32
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e, 0]
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e + 4, 0]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_warp_col = b_seg >> 2
+            b_local_seg = b_seg & 3
+            b_lane_base = b_local_seg * 8
+            b_lane_group = b_row >> 2
+            b_lane_off = (b_row & 3) + (b_lane_group & 1) * 4
+            b_frag_half = b_lane_group >> 1
+            for e in S.range(8):
+                b_lane = b_lane_base + e
+                b_lane_frags[b_warp_col, b_lane, b_frag_half * 4 + b_lane_off] = b_frag[e, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        m_a = S.view(a_lane_frags[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_lane_frags[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = warp_col_base + lane_col
+        out_row = warp_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+        if out_row < BATCH_SIZE and out_col < OUT_FEATURES:
+            v = (acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)) * S.convert(SCALE[out_col], S.f32)
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),

+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),

+        var = VAR[col]

+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    SCALE: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    warp_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)
+
+    a_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            a_warp_row = a_row >> 5
+            a_lane_row = a_row & 31
+            a_lane_hi = a_lane_row + 32
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e, 0]
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e + 4, 0]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_warp_col = b_seg >> 2
+            b_local_seg = b_seg & 3
+            b_lane_base = b_local_seg * 8
+            b_lane_group = b_row >> 2
+            b_lane_off = (b_row & 3) + (b_lane_group & 1) * 4
+            b_frag_half = b_lane_group >> 1
+            for e in S.range(8):
+                b_lane = b_lane_base + e
+                b_lane_frags[b_warp_col, b_lane, b_frag_half * 4 + b_lane_off] = b_frag[e, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        m_a = S.view(a_lane_frags[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_lane_frags[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = warp_col_base + lane_col
+        out_row = warp_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+        if out_row < BATCH_SIZE and out_col < OUT_FEATURES:
+            v = (acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)) * S.convert(SCALE[out_col], S.f32)
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+
 
 @substrate.jit

+def bn_stats_kernel(

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    VAR: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1) * 4 + (tid >> 6)
+    col = S.block_id(0) * 64 + (tid & 63)
+    if row < BATCH_SIZE and col < OUT_FEATURES:
+        mean = MEAN[col]
+        var = VAR[col]
         denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
-            v = (S.convert(Y[i, j], S.f32) - mean) / denom
-            v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[j], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[j], S.f32)
-            Y[i, j] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+        v = (S.convert(Y[row, col], S.f32) - mean) / denom
+        v = v * S.convert(BN_WEIGHT[col], S.f32) + S.convert(BN_BIAS[col], S.f32)
+        OUT[row, col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

codex
The NaNs come from leaving part of the B lane fragments undefined. I’m fixing that so the upper 32 lanes carry K rows `4..7` and `12..15`, matching the same low/high-lane split as the accumulator layout.

+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")
+
+        x_in = x.contiguous()
+        w_t = self._cached_contiguous("w_t", self.gemm.weight, transpose=True)
+        bias = self._cached_contiguous("bias", self.gemm.bias)
+        scale = self._cached_contiguous("scale", self.scale)
+        bn_w = self._cached_contiguous("bn_w", self.bn.weight)
+        bn_b = self._cached_contiguous("bn_b", self.bn.bias)
+
+        gemm_out = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        mean = torch.empty((OUT_FEATURES,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
+        var = torch.empty((OUT_FEATURES,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
+        out = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+

+        bn_stats_kernel[_launch_bn_stats](gemm_out, mean, var)
+        bn_apply_kernel[_launch_bn_apply](gemm_out, mean, var, bn_w, bn_b, out)
+        return out

 import torch.nn as nn
 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S
-SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951
 
-def _launch():

+SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951
 BATCH_SIZE = 1024
 IN_FEATURES = 8192
 OUT_FEATURES = 8192
 EPS = 1e-05
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+A_TILE_RANGE_BYTES = BLOCK_M * BLOCK_K * 2
+B_TILE_RANGE_BYTES = BLOCK_K * BLOCK_N * 2
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2

+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_bn_stats():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // 256, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_bn_apply():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // 64, BATCH_SIZE // 4, 1), (256, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_scale_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    SCALE: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    warp_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)
+
+    a_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            a_warp_row = a_row >> 5
+            a_lane_row = a_row & 31
+            a_lane_hi = a_lane_row + 32
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e, 0]
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e + 4, 0]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_warp_col = b_seg >> 2
+            b_local_seg = b_seg & 3
+            b_lane_base = b_local_seg * 8
+            b_lane_hi = ((b_row >> 2) & 1) * 32
+            b_frag_half = b_row >> 3
+            b_lane_off = b_row & 3
+            for e in S.range(8):
+                b_lane = b_lane_base + e + b_lane_hi
+                b_lane_frags[b_warp_col, b_lane, b_frag_half * 4 + b_lane_off] = b_frag[e, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        m_a = S.view(a_lane_frags[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_lane_frags[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = warp_col_base + lane_col
+        out_row = warp_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+        if out_row < BATCH_SIZE and out_col < OUT_FEATURES:
+            v = (acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)) * S.convert(SCALE[out_col], S.f32)
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    VAR: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    row = S.block_id(1) * 4 + (tid >> 6)
+    col = S.block_id(0) * 64 + (tid & 63)
+    if row < BATCH_SIZE and col < OUT_FEATURES:
+        mean = MEAN[col]
+        var = VAR[col]

+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1))

+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // 256, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))

+def _launch_bn_apply():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // 64, BATCH_SIZE // 4, 1), (256, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_scale_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    SCALE: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    warp_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)
+
+    a_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            a_warp_row = a_row >> 5
+            a_lane_row = a_row & 31
+            a_lane_hi = a_lane_row + 32
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e, 0]
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e + 4, 0]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_warp_col = b_seg >> 2
+            b_local_seg = b_seg & 3
+            b_lane_base = b_local_seg * 8
+            b_lane_hi = ((b_row >> 2) & 1) * 32
+            b_frag_half = b_row >> 3
+            b_lane_off = b_row & 3
+            for e in S.range(8):
+                b_lane = b_lane_base + e + b_lane_hi
+                b_lane_frags[b_warp_col, b_lane, b_frag_half * 4 + b_lane_off] = b_frag[e, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        m_a = S.view(a_lane_frags[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_lane_frags[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = warp_col_base + lane_col
+        out_row = warp_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+        if out_row < BATCH_SIZE and out_col < OUT_FEATURES:
+            v = (acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)) * S.convert(SCALE[out_col], S.f32)
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)
+

 import substrate.language as S

+SQRT_2 = 1.4142135623730951
 BATCH_SIZE = 1024
 IN_FEATURES = 8192
 OUT_FEATURES = 8192
 EPS = 1e-05
+BLOCK_M = 64
+BLOCK_N = 64
+BLOCK_K = 16
+WARP_SIZE = 64
+NUM_WARPS = 4
+THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
+A_TILE_RANGE_BYTES = BLOCK_M * BLOCK_K * 2
+B_TILE_RANGE_BYTES = BLOCK_K * BLOCK_N * 2
+X_RANGE_BYTES = BATCH_SIZE * IN_FEATURES * 2
+W_RANGE_BYTES = IN_FEATURES * OUT_FEATURES * 2

+
+def _launch_gemm():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (THREADS, 1, 1))

+def _launch_bn_stats():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // 256, 1, 1), (256, 1, 1))
+
+
+def _launch_bn_apply():
+    return ((OUT_FEATURES // 64, BATCH_SIZE // 4, 1), (256, 1, 1))

+@substrate.jit
+def gemm_scale_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    SCALE: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    warp_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)
+
+    a_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            a_warp_row = a_row >> 5
+            a_lane_row = a_row & 31
+            a_lane_hi = a_lane_row + 32
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e, 0]
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e + 4, 0]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_warp_col = b_seg >> 2
+            b_local_seg = b_seg & 3
+            b_lane_base = b_local_seg * 8
+            b_lane_hi = ((b_row >> 2) & 1) * 32
+            b_frag_half = b_row >> 3
+            b_lane_off = b_row & 3
+            for e in S.range(8):
+                b_lane = b_lane_base + e + b_lane_hi
+                b_lane_frags[b_warp_col, b_lane, b_frag_half * 4 + b_lane_off] = b_frag[e, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        m_a = S.view(a_lane_frags[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_lane_frags[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = warp_col_base + lane_col
+        out_row = warp_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+        if out_row < BATCH_SIZE and out_col < OUT_FEATURES:
+            v = (acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(BIAS0[out_col], S.f32)) * S.convert(SCALE[out_col], S.f32)
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(v, S.bf16)

The remaining error is small enough that it looks like parameter precision, not tile layout. I’m keeping the MFMA path and switching the scalar epilogue/BN parameters to `f32`, which is closer to how the original PyTorch module executes.

+def gemm_scale_mfma_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    W: S.Tensor((IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+    BIAS0: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    SCALE: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.f32),
+    x_range_bytes: S.i32,
+    w_range_bytes: S.i32,
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    lane = tid & 63
+    warp_id = tid >> 6
+    warp_row = warp_id >> 1
+    warp_col = warp_id & 1
+
+    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
+    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
+    warp_row_base = block_row + warp_row * 32
+    warp_col_base = block_col + warp_col * 32
+
+    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, x_range_bytes)
+    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, w_range_bytes)
+
+    a_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+    b_lane_frags = S.make_shared((2, 64, 8), S.bf16)
+
+    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)
+    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
+
+    for k0 in S.range(0, IN_FEATURES, BLOCK_K):
+        if tid < 128:
+            a_chunk = tid
+            a_row = a_chunk >> 1
+            a_half = a_chunk & 1
+            x_elem_offset = (block_row + a_row) * IN_FEATURES + k0 + a_half * 8
+            x_byte_offset = S.convert(x_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero, x_byte_offset, 0)
+            a_frag = S.view(a_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            a_warp_row = a_row >> 5
+            a_lane_row = a_row & 31
+            a_lane_hi = a_lane_row + 32
+            for e in S.range(4):
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_row, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e, 0]
+                a_lane_frags[a_warp_row, a_lane_hi, a_half * 4 + e] = a_frag[e + 4, 0]
+        else:
+            b_chunk = tid - 128
+            b_row = b_chunk >> 3
+            b_seg = b_chunk & 7
+            w_elem_offset = (k0 + b_row) * OUT_FEATURES + block_col + b_seg * 8
+            w_byte_offset = S.convert(w_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
+            b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero, w_byte_offset, 0)
+            b_frag = S.view(b_pack, S.Tensor((8, 1), S.bf16))
+            b_warp_col = b_seg >> 2
+            b_local_seg = b_seg & 3
+            b_lane_base = b_local_seg * 8
+            b_lane_hi = ((b_row >> 2) & 1) * 32
+            b_frag_half = b_row >> 3
+            b_lane_off = b_row & 3
+            for e in S.range(8):
+                b_lane = b_lane_base + e + b_lane_hi
+                b_lane_frags[b_warp_col, b_lane, b_frag_half * 4 + b_lane_off] = b_frag[e, 0]
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+        m_a = S.view(a_lane_frags[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+        m_b = S.view(b_lane_frags[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], acc)
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], acc)
+
+        S.syncthreads()
+
+    lane_col = lane & 31
+    lane_row_quad = lane >> 5
+    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
+        out_col = warp_col_base + lane_col
+        out_row = warp_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx >> 2) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx & 3)
+        if out_row < BATCH_SIZE and out_col < OUT_FEATURES:
+            Y[out_row, out_col] = (acc[acc_idx] + BIAS0[out_col]) * SCALE[out_col]
+

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_stats_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.f32),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    VAR: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+):

+    if col < OUT_FEATURES:

+        for row in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
+            mean += Y[row, col]

         var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
-        for i in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):

+@substrate.jit
+def bn_apply_kernel(
+    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.f32),
+    MEAN: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    VAR: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_WEIGHT: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    BN_BIAS: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
+    OUT: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
+):

+        var = VAR[col]

+def bn_apply_kernel(
